text,Image:livre5,"The Story of the Toad King

A long time ago there lived an evil king. His face was so repulsive that he was known as the Toad King. One fine day a masked man presented himself at court and spoke these words: “Good day, wicked ruler. Go from here, and leave your people in peace, or taste the blade of my sword.”

The king replied, “I am the king, and you are my subjects. It is not for you to oppose my will.” So the masked man raised his sword and slew the king.

The End"
